## completeCartWorkflow

This workflow completes a cart.

### Steps

### Hooks

## validateExistingPaymentCollectionStep

This step validates that a cart doesn't have a payment collection.

## updateTaxLinesWorkflow

This workflow updates a cart's tax lines.

### Steps

<WorkflowDiagram workflow={{"name":"updateTaxLinesWorkflow","steps":[{"type":"step","name":"retrieveCartWithLinksStep","description":"This step retrieves a cart's details with its linked records.","link":"../core_flows.Steps_Cart/page.mdx#retrievecartwithlinksstep","depth":1},{"type":"step","name":"getItemTaxLinesStep","description":"This step retrieves the tax lines of the specified line items in a cart.","link":"../core_flows.Steps_Cart/page.mdx#getitemtaxlinesstep","depth":2},{"type":"step","name":"setTaxLinesForItemsStep","description":"This step sets the tax lines of shipping methods and line items in a cart.","link":"../core_flows.Steps_Cart/page.mdx#settaxlinesforitemsstep","depth":3}]}} />
